INNER JOIN "Cart" AS c0 ON c."CartId" = c0."CartId"
INNER JOIN "ProductVariant" AS p ON c."ProductVariantId" = p."ProductVariantId"
INNER JOIN "Product" AS p0 ON p."ProductId" = p0."ProductId"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT i."InventoryId", i."AddressId", i."AvailableQuantity", i."ProductVariantId", i."ReservedQuantity", i."UpdatedAt", a."AddressId" AS "AddressId0", a."AddressLine", a."City", a."ContactName", a."ContactPhoneNumber", a."Country", a."CreatedAt", a."IsDefault", a."LandMark", a."PinCode", a."State", a."UpdatedAt" AS "UpdatedAt0", a."UserId"

    INNER JOIN "Address" AS a ON i."AddressId" = a."AddressId"
) AS s ON p."ProductVariantId" = s."ProductVariantId"
WHERE c0."UserId" = @userId
ORDER BY c."CartItemsId", c0."CartId", p."ProductVariantId", p0."ProductId", s."InventoryId"
